  <div class="container slp-text-center slp-mt-48 slp-py-48 install-header"> 
   <h1 class="slp-text-3xl slp-font-normal md:slp-text-5xl">Install self-managed GitLab</h1> 
   <p class="slp-my-32 slp-text-md slp-font-normal md:slp-text-lg">You can download, install and maintain your own GitLab instance.</p> 
   <p class="margin-left-none"> Want to try GitLab Ultimate for 30 days? <a href="/free-trial/self-managed/" class="slp-text-ui-secondary-dark">Get your free trial ?</a> </p> 
  </div> 
  <div id="content" role="main"> 
   <div class="cards-section cards-section-grey"> 
    <div class="container slp-container"> 
     <div class="method omnibus"> 
      <div class="method-content"> 
       <p class="slp-text-center slp-text-md slp-font-normal">Recommended installation</p> 
       <h2 class="slp-text-center slp-text-xl slp-font-normal md:slp-text-3xl" id="omnibus">Official Linux package</h2> 
       <p class="slp-text-center"> Linux installation is quicker to install, easier to upgrade and contains features to enhance reliability not found in other methods. Install via a single package (also known as Omnibus) that bundles all the different services and tools required to run GitLab. At least 4 GB of RAM is recommended. </p>

          <h4 class="tile-title"> Ubuntu </h4> 
          <p> 16.04 LTS, 18.04 LTS, 20.04 LTS </p>
          <div class="tile-link slp-text-ui-secondary-dark">
            Install instructions + 
          </div> 
          <p></p> 
         </div> </a> 
        <li class="distro-content js-distro-content hidden distro-content-1" id="ubuntu"> 
         <div class="js-platform-ce js-install-instructions"> 
          <p></p> 
          <p class="alert alert-info">For Ubuntu 20.04, <code>arm64</code> packages are also available.</p> 
          <h4> 1. Install and configure the necessary dependencies </h4> 
          <pre class="command">sudo apt-get install -y curl openssh-server ca-certificates tzdata perl
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo apt-get install -y curl openssh-server ca-certificates tzdata perl


" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p> Next, install Postfix to send notification emails. If you want to use another solution to send emails please skip this step and <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/smtp.html">configure an external SMTP server</a> after GitLab has been installed. </p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo apt-get install -y postfix
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo apt-get install -y postfix

" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p> During Postfix installation a configuration screen may appear. Select 'Internet Site' and press enter. Use your server's external DNS for 'mail name' and press enter. If additional screens appear, continue to press enter to accept the defaults. </p> 
          <h4> 2. Add the GitLab package repository and install the package </h4> 
          <p> Add the GitLab package repository. </p> 
          <pre class="command">curl -sS https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/gitlab-ce/script.deb.sh | sudo bash
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="curl -sS https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/gitlab-ce/script.deb.sh | sudo bash
" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>Next, install the GitLab package. Make sure you have correctly <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">set up your DNS</a>, and change <code>https://gitlab.example.com</code> to the URL at which you want to access your GitLab instance. Installation will automatically configure and start GitLab at that URL.</p> 
          <p>For <code>https://</code> URLs, GitLab will automatically <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/ssl.html#lets-encrypthttpsletsencryptorg-integration">request a certificate with Let's Encrypt</a>, which requires inbound HTTP access and a <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">valid hostname</a>. You can also <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/nginx.html#manually-configuring-https">use your own certificate</a> or just use <code>http://</code> (without <code>s</code>).</p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo EXTERNAL_URL="https://gitlab.example.com" apt-get install gitlab-ce
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo EXTERNAL_URL=&quot;https://gitlab.example.com&quot; apt-get install gitlab-ce
" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <h4> 3. Browse to the hostname and login </h4> 
          <p>On your first visit, you'll be redirected to a password reset screen. Provide the password for the initial administrator account and you will be redirected back to the login screen. Use the default account's username <code>root</code> to login.</p> 
          <p>See our <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/README.html#installation-and-configuration-using-omnibus-package">documentation for detailed instructions on installing and configuration</a>.</p> 
          <h4> 4. Set up your communication preferences </h4> 
          <p> Visit our <a href="/company/preference-center/">email subscription preference center</a> to let us know when to communicate with you. We have an explicit email opt-in policy so you have complete control over what and how often we send you emails. </p> 
          <p> Twice a month, we send out the GitLab news you need to know, including new features, integrations, docs, and behind the scenes stories from our dev teams. For critical security updates related to bugs and system performance, sign up for our dedicated security newsletter. </p> 
          <p class="alert alert-warning"><strong>Important note:</strong> If you do not opt-in to the security newsletter, you will not receive security alerts.</p> 
          <h4> 5. Recommended next steps </h4> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>After completing your installation, consider the <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/install/#next-steps">recommended next steps</a>, including <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/security/README.html#securing-your-gitlab-installation">authentication options and sign-up restrictions</a>.</p> 
          <div class="display-extra-links"> <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/"> Troubleshooting </a> <a href="http://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/manual_install.html"> Manual installation </a> <a href="/install/ce-or-ee/?distro=ubuntu"> CE or EE </a> 
          </div> 
         </div>

          <p> During Postfix installation a configuration screen may appear. Select 'Internet Site' and press enter. Use your server's external DNS for 'mail name' and press enter. If additional screens appear, continue to press enter to accept the defaults. </p> 
          <h4> 2. Add the GitLab package repository and install the package </h4> 
          <p> Add the GitLab package repository. </p> 
          <pre class="command">curl -sS https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/gitlab-ce/script.deb.sh | sudo bash
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="curl -sS https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/gitlab-ce/script.deb.sh | sudo bash
" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>Next, install the GitLab package. Make sure you have correctly <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">set up your DNS</a>, and change <code>https://gitlab.example.com</code> to the URL at which you want to access your GitLab instance. Installation will automatically configure and start GitLab at that URL.</p> 
          <p>For <code>https://</code> URLs, GitLab will automatically <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/ssl.html#lets-encrypthttpsletsencryptorg-integration">request a certificate with Let's Encrypt</a>, which requires inbound HTTP access and a <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">valid hostname</a>. You can also <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/nginx.html#manually-configuring-https">use your own certificate</a> or just use <code>http://</code> (without <code>s</code>).</p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo EXTERNAL_URL="https://gitlab.example.com" apt-get install gitlab-ce
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo EXTERNAL_URL=&quot;https://gitlab.example.com&quot; apt-get install gitlab-ce
" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <h4> 3. Browse to the hostname and login </h4> 
          <p>On your first visit, you'll be redirected to a password reset screen. Provide the password for the initial administrator account and you will be redirected back to the login screen. Use the default account's username <code>root</code> to login.</p> 
          <p>See our <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/README.html#installation-and-configuration-using-omnibus-package">documentation for detailed instructions on installing and configuration</a>.</p> 
          <h4> 4. Set up your communication preferences </h4> 
          <p> Visit our <a href="/company/preference-center/">email subscription preference center</a> to let us know when to communicate with you. We have an explicit email opt-in policy so you have complete control over what and how often we send you emails. </p> 
          <p> Twice a month, we send out the GitLab news you need to know, including new features, integrations, docs, and behind the scenes stories from our dev teams. For critical security updates related to bugs and system performance, sign up for our dedicated security newsletter. </p> 
          <p class="alert alert-warning"><strong>Important note:</strong> If you do not opt-in to the security newsletter, you will not receive security alerts.</p> 
          <h4> 5. Recommended next steps </h4> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>After completing your installation, consider the <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/install/#next-steps">recommended next steps</a>, including <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/security/README.html#securing-your-gitlab-installation">authentication options and sign-up restrictions</a>.</p>

sudo firewall-cmd --permanent --add-service=https
sudo systemctl reload firewalld

          <h4> 2. Add the GitLab package repository and install the package </h4> 
          <p> Add the GitLab package repository. </p> 
          <pre class="command">curl https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/gitlab-ee/script.rpm.sh | sudo bash
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="curl https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/gitlab-ee/script.rpm.sh | sudo bash
" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>Next, install the GitLab package. Make sure you have correctly <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">set up your DNS</a>, and change <code>https://gitlab.example.com</code> to the URL at which you want to access your GitLab instance. Installation will automatically configure and start GitLab at that URL.</p> 
          <p>For <code>https://</code> URLs, GitLab will automatically <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/ssl.html#lets-encrypthttpsletsencryptorg-integration">request a certificate with Let's Encrypt</a>, which requires inbound HTTP access and a <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">valid hostname</a>. You can also <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/nginx.html#manually-configuring-https">use your own certificate</a> or just use <code>http://</code> (without <code>s</code>).</p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo EXTERNAL_URL="https://gitlab.example.com" dnf install -y gitlab-ee<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo EXTERNAL_URL=&quot;https://gitlab.example.com&quot; dnf install -y gitlab-ee" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <h4> 3. Browse to the hostname and login </h4> 
          <p>On your first visit, you'll be redirected to a password reset screen. Provide the password for the initial administrator account and you will be redirected back to the login screen. Use the default account's username <code>root</code> to login.</p> 
          <p>See our <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/README.html#installation-and-configuration-using-omnibus-package">documentation for detailed instructions on installing and configuration</a>.</p> 
          <h4> 4. Set up your communication preferences </h4> 
          <p> Visit our <a href="/company/preference-center/">email subscription preference center</a> to let us know when to communicate with you. We have an explicit email opt-in policy so you have complete control over what and how often we send you emails. </p> 
          <p> Twice a month, we send out the GitLab news you need to know, including new features, integrations, docs, and behind the scenes stories from our dev teams. For critical security updates related to bugs and system performance, sign up for our dedicated security newsletter. </p> 
          <p class="alert alert-warning"><strong>Important note:</strong> If you do not opt-in to the security newsletter, you will not receive security alerts.</p> 
          <h4> 5. Recommended next steps </h4> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>After completing your installation, consider the <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/install/#next-steps">recommended next steps</a>, including <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/security/README.html#securing-your-gitlab-installation">authentication options and sign-up restrictions</a>.</p>

         <div class="js-platform-ce js-install-instructions"> 
          <h4> 1. Install and configure the necessary dependencies </h4> 
          <p>On CentOS 7, the commands below will also open HTTP, HTTPS and SSH access in the system firewall. This is an optional step, and you can skip it if you intend to access GitLab only from your local network.</p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo yum install -y curl policycoreutils-python openssh-server openssh-clients perl
sudo systemctl enable sshd
sudo systemctl start sshd
sudo firewall-cmd --permanent --add-service=http
sudo firewall-cmd --permanent --add-service=https
sudo systemctl reload firewalld
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo yum install -y curl policycoreutils-python openssh-server openssh-clients perl
sudo systemctl enable sshd
sudo systemctl start sshd

sudo firewall-cmd --permanent --add-service=http
sudo firewall-cmd --permanent --add-service=https
sudo systemctl reload firewalld

" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p> Next, install Postfix to send notification emails. If you want to use another solution to send emails please skip this step and <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/smtp.html">configure an external SMTP server</a> after GitLab has been installed. </p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo yum install postfix
sudo systemctl enable postfix
sudo systemctl start postfix
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo yum install postfix
sudo systemctl enable postfix
sudo systemctl start postfix

" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p> During Postfix installation a configuration screen may appear. Select 'Internet Site' and press enter. Use your server's external DNS for 'mail name' and press enter. If additional screens appear, continue to press enter to accept the defaults. </p> 
          <h4> 2. Add the GitLab package repository and install the package </h4> 
          <p> Add the GitLab package repository. </p> 
          <pre class="command">curl -sS https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/gitlab-ce/script.rpm.sh | sudo bash
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="curl -sS https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/gitlab-ce/script.rpm.sh | sudo bash
" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>Next, install the GitLab package. Make sure you have correctly <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">set up your DNS</a>, and change <code>https://gitlab.example.com</code> to the URL at which you want to access your GitLab instance. Installation will automatically configure and start GitLab at that URL.</p> 
          <p>For <code>https://</code> URLs, GitLab will automatically <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/ssl.html#lets-encrypthttpsletsencryptorg-integration">request a certificate with Let's Encrypt</a>, which requires inbound HTTP access and a <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">valid hostname</a>. You can also <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/nginx.html#manually-configuring-https">use your own certificate</a> or just use <code>http://</code> (without <code>s</code>).</p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo EXTERNAL_URL="https://gitlab.example.com" yum install -y gitlab-ce
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo EXTERNAL_URL=&quot;https://gitlab.example.com&quot; yum install -y gitlab-ce
" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <h4> 3. Browse to the hostname and login </h4> 
          <p>On your first visit, you'll be redirected to a password reset screen. Provide the password for the initial administrator account and you will be redirected back to the login screen. Use the default account's username <code>root</code> to login.</p> 
          <p>See our <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/README.html#installation-and-configuration-using-omnibus-package">documentation for detailed instructions on installing and configuration</a>.</p> 
          <h4> 4. Set up your communication preferences </h4> 
          <p> Visit our <a href="/company/preference-center/">email subscription preference center</a> to let us know when to communicate with you. We have an explicit email opt-in policy so you have complete control over what and how often we send you emails. </p> 
          <p> Twice a month, we send out the GitLab news you need to know, including new features, integrations, docs, and behind the scenes stories from our dev teams. For critical security updates related to bugs and system performance, sign up for our dedicated security newsletter. </p> 
          <p class="alert alert-warning"><strong>Important note:</strong> If you do not opt-in to the security newsletter, you will not receive security alerts.</p> 
          <h4> 5. Recommended next steps </h4> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>After completing your installation, consider the <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/install/#next-steps">recommended next steps</a>, including <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/security/README.html#securing-your-gitlab-installation">authentication options and sign-up restrictions</a>.</p>

          <h4 class="tile-title"> OpenSUSE Leap 15.1, 15.2 </h4> 
          <p> and SUSE Linux Enterprise Server 12.2, 12.5 </p>

            Install instructions +

         </div> </a> 
        <li class="distro-content js-distro-content hidden distro-content-5" id="opensuse-leap-15-1-15-2"> 
         <div class="js-platform-ce js-install-instructions"> 
          <p></p> 
          <p class="alert alert-info">For OpenSuse, <code>arm64</code> packages are also available.</p> 
          <h4> 1. Install and configure the necessary dependencies </h4> 
          <p>On OpenSUSE, the commands below will also open HTTP, HTTPS and SSH access in the system firewall. This is an optional step, and you can skip it if you intend to access GitLab only from your local network.</p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo zypper install curl openssh perl
sudo systemctl enable sshd
sudo systemctl start sshd
sudo firewall-cmd --permanent --add-service=http
sudo firewall-cmd --permanent --add-service=https
sudo systemctl reload firewalld
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo zypper install curl openssh perl
sudo systemctl enable sshd
sudo systemctl start sshd

sudo firewall-cmd --permanent --add-service=http
sudo firewall-cmd --permanent --add-service=https
sudo systemctl reload firewalld

" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p> Next, install Postfix to send notification emails. If you want to use another solution to send emails please skip this step and <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/smtp.html">configure an external SMTP server</a> after GitLab has been installed. </p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo zypper install postfix
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo zypper install postfix

" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p> During Postfix installation a configuration screen may appear. Select 'Internet Site' and press enter. Use your server's external DNS for 'mail name' and press enter. If additional screens appear, continue to press enter to accept the defaults. </p> 
          <h4> 2. Add the GitLab package repository and install the package </h4> 
          <p> Add the GitLab package repository. </p> 
          <pre class="command">curl -sS https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/gitlab-ce/script.rpm.sh | sudo bash
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="curl -sS https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/gitlab-ce/script.rpm.sh | sudo bash
" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>Next, install the GitLab package. Make sure you have correctly <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">set up your DNS</a>, and change <code>https://gitlab.example.com</code> to the URL at which you want to access your GitLab instance. Installation will automatically configure and start GitLab at that URL.</p> 
          <p>For <code>https://</code> URLs, GitLab will automatically <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/ssl.html#lets-encrypthttpsletsencryptorg-integration">request a certificate with Let's Encrypt</a>, which requires inbound HTTP access and a <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">valid hostname</a>. You can also <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/nginx.html#manually-configuring-https">use your own certificate</a> or just use <code>http://</code> (without <code>s</code>).</p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo EXTERNAL_URL="https://gitlab.example.com" zypper install gitlab-ce
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo EXTERNAL_URL=&quot;https://gitlab.example.com&quot; zypper install gitlab-ce
" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <h4> 3. Browse to the hostname and login </h4> 
          <p>On your first visit, you'll be redirected to a password reset screen. Provide the password for the initial administrator account and you will be redirected back to the login screen. Use the default account's username <code>root</code> to login.</p> 
          <p>See our <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/README.html#installation-and-configuration-using-omnibus-package">documentation for detailed instructions on installing and configuration</a>.</p> 
          <h4> 4. Set up your communication preferences </h4> 
          <p> Visit our <a href="/company/preference-center/">email subscription preference center</a> to let us know when to communicate with you. We have an explicit email opt-in policy so you have complete control over what and how often we send you emails. </p> 
          <p> Twice a month, we send out the GitLab news you need to know, including new features, integrations, docs, and behind the scenes stories from our dev teams. For critical security updates related to bugs and system performance, sign up for our dedicated security newsletter. </p> 
          <p class="alert alert-warning"><strong>Important note:</strong> If you do not opt-in to the security newsletter, you will not receive security alerts.</p> 
          <h4> 5. Recommended next steps </h4> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>After completing your installation, consider the <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/install/#next-steps">recommended next steps</a>, including <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/security/README.html#securing-your-gitlab-installation">authentication options and sign-up restrictions</a>.</p> 
          <div class="display-extra-links"> <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/"> Troubleshooting </a> <a href="http://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/manual_install.html"> Manual installation </a> <a href="/install/ce-or-ee/?distro=opensuse-leap-15-1-15-2"> CE or EE </a> 
          </div> 
         </div>

          <p></p> 
          <p class="alert alert-info">For OpenSuse, <code>arm64</code> packages are also available.</p> 
          <h4> 1. Install and configure the necessary dependencies </h4> 
          <p>On OpenSUSE, the commands below will also open HTTP, HTTPS and SSH access in the system firewall. This is an optional step, and you can skip it if you intend to access GitLab only from your local network.</p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo zypper install curl openssh perl
sudo systemctl enable sshd
sudo systemctl start sshd
sudo firewall-cmd --permanent --add-service=http
sudo firewall-cmd --permanent --add-service=https

sudo firewall-cmd --permanent --add-service=https
sudo systemctl reload firewalld

" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p> Next, install Postfix to send notification emails. If you want to use another solution to send emails please skip this step and <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/smtp.html">configure an external SMTP server</a> after GitLab has been installed. </p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo zypper install postfix
sudo systemctl enable postfix
sudo systemctl start postfix
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo zypper install postfix
sudo systemctl enable postfix
sudo systemctl start postfix

" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p> During Postfix installation a configuration screen may appear. Select 'Internet Site' and press enter. Use your server's external DNS for 'mail name' and press enter. If additional screens appear, continue to press enter to accept the defaults. </p> 
          <h4> 2. Add the GitLab package repository and install the package </h4> 
          <p> Add the GitLab package repository. </p> 
          <pre class="command">curl -sS https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/gitlab-ee/script.rpm.sh | sudo bash
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="curl -sS https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/gitlab-ee/script.rpm.sh | sudo bash
" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>Next, install the GitLab package. Make sure you have correctly <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">set up your DNS</a>, and change <code>https://gitlab.example.com</code> to the URL at which you want to access your GitLab instance. Installation will automatically configure and start GitLab at that URL.</p> 
          <p>For <code>https://</code> URLs, GitLab will automatically <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/ssl.html#lets-encrypthttpsletsencryptorg-integration">request a certificate with Let's Encrypt</a>, which requires inbound HTTP access and a <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">valid hostname</a>. You can also <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/nginx.html#manually-configuring-https">use your own certificate</a> or just use <code>http://</code> (without <code>s</code>).</p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo EXTERNAL_URL="https://gitlab.example.com" zypper install gitlab-ee<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo EXTERNAL_URL=&quot;https://gitlab.example.com&quot; zypper install gitlab-ee" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <h4> 3. Browse to the hostname and login </h4> 
          <p>On your first visit, you'll be redirected to a password reset screen. Provide the password for the initial administrator account and you will be redirected back to the login screen. Use the default account's username <code>root</code> to login.</p> 
          <p>See our <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/README.html#installation-and-configuration-using-omnibus-package">documentation for detailed instructions on installing and configuration</a>.</p> 
          <h4> 4. Set up your communication preferences </h4> 
          <p> Visit our <a href="/company/preference-center/">email subscription preference center</a> to let us know when to communicate with you. We have an explicit email opt-in policy so you have complete control over what and how often we send you emails. </p> 
          <p> Twice a month, we send out the GitLab news you need to know, including new features, integrations, docs, and behind the scenes stories from our dev teams. For critical security updates related to bugs and system performance, sign up for our dedicated security newsletter. </p> 
          <p class="alert alert-warning"><strong>Important note:</strong> If you do not opt-in to the security newsletter, you will not receive security alerts.</p> 
          <h4> 5. Recommended next steps </h4> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>After completing your installation, consider the <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/install/#next-steps">recommended next steps</a>, including <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/ee/security/README.html#securing-your-gitlab-installation">authentication options and sign-up restrictions</a>.</p>

          <h4 class="tile-title"> Raspberry Pi OS </h4>

         <div class="js-platform-ce js-install-instructions"> 
          <p></p> 
          <p class="alert alert-info">Raspberry Pi 4 with at least 4GB is recommended. Only 32bit (<code>armhf</code>) is supported at this point. 64 bit (<code>arm64</code>) is <a href="https://gitlab.com/groups/gitlab-org/-/epics/2370">on its way</a>.</p> 
          <h4> 1. Install and configure the necessary dependencies </h4> 
          <pre class="command">sudo apt-get install curl openssh-server ca-certificates apt-transport-https perl
curl https://packages.gitlab.com/gpg.key | sudo apt-key add -
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo apt-get install curl openssh-server ca-certificates apt-transport-https perl
curl https://packages.gitlab.com/gpg.key | sudo apt-key add -


" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p> Next, install Postfix to send notification emails. If you want to use another solution to send emails please skip this step and <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/smtp.html">configure an external SMTP server</a> after GitLab has been installed. </p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo apt-get install -y postfix
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo apt-get install -y postfix

" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p> During Postfix installation a configuration screen may appear. Select 'Internet Site' and press enter. Use your server's external DNS for 'mail name' and press enter. If additional screens appear, continue to press enter to accept the defaults. </p> 
          <h4> 2. Add the GitLab package repository and install the package </h4> 
          <p> Add the GitLab package repository. </p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo curl -sS https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/raspberry-pi2/script.deb.sh | sudo bash

<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo curl -sS https://packages.gitlab.com/install/repositories/gitlab/raspberry-pi2/script.deb.sh | sudo bash

" data-placement="top" data-toggle="tooltip" title="Copy to clipboard" type="button">
<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <p></p> 
          <p>Next, install the GitLab package. Make sure you have correctly <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">set up your DNS</a>, and change <code>https://gitlab.example.com</code> to the URL at which you want to access your GitLab instance. Installation will automatically configure and start GitLab at that URL.</p> 
          <p>For <code>https://</code> URLs, GitLab will automatically <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/ssl.html#lets-encrypthttpsletsencryptorg-integration">request a certificate with Let's Encrypt</a>, which requires inbound HTTP access and a <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/dns.html">valid hostname</a>. You can also <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/settings/nginx.html#manually-configuring-https">use your own certificate</a> or just use <code>http://</code> (without <code>s</code>).</p> 
          <pre class="command">sudo EXTERNAL_URL="https://gitlab.example.com" apt-get install gitlab-ce
<button aria-label="Copy to clipboard" class="btn copy-btn js-copy-btn" data-clipboard-text="sudo EXTERNAL_URL=&quot;https://gitlab.example.com&quot; apt-get install gitlab-ce

<i class="fa fa-clipboard"></i>
</button></pre> 
          <h4> 3. Browse to the hostname and login </h4> 
          <p>On your first visit, you'll be redirected to a password reset screen. Provide the password for the initial administrator account and you will be redirected back to the login screen. Use the default account's username <code>root</code> to login.</p> 
          <p>See our <a href="https://docs.gitlab.com/omnibus/README.html#installation-and-configuration-using-omnibus-package">documentation for detailed instructions on installing and configuration</a>.</p>

          <p> Visit our <a href="/company/preference-center/">email subscription preference center</a> to let us know when to communicate with you. We have an explicit email opt-in policy so you have complete control over what and how often we send you emails. </p> 
          <p> Twice a month, we send out the GitLab news you need to know, including new features, integrations, docs, and behind the scenes stories from our dev teams. For critical security updates related to bugs and system performance, sign up for our dedicated security newsletter. </p> 
          <p class="alert alert-warning"><strong>Important note:</strong> If you do not opt-in to the security newsletter, you will not receive security alerts.</p>
